is_crazy_COG_and_technocracy_against_GER = {
	enable = {
		num_divisions > 0
		OR = {
			AND = {
				original_tag = COG
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Simon Kimbangu"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_completed_focus = COG_empire_of_black_christ
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = GER }
				has_completed_focus = concept_of_technate
				has_government = technocracy
			}
		}
		GER = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = "GER"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = "GER"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = prepare_for_war
		id = "GER"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = declare_war
		id = "GER"
		value = 500
	}
}

		OR = {
			AND = {
				original_tag = COG
				has_country_leader = {
					name = "Simon Kimbangu"
					ruling_only = yes
				}
				has_completed_focus = COG_empire_of_black_christ
			}
			AND = {
				NOT = { tag = CRO }
				has_completed_focus = concept_of_technate
				has_government = technocracy
			}
		}
		CRO = {
			is_neighbor_of = ROOT
			NOT = {
				is_in_faction_with = ROOT
				is_subject_of = ROOT
			}
		}
	}
	abort_when_not_enabled = yes
	
	ai_strategy = {
		type = antagonize
		id = "CRO"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = conquer
		id = "CRO"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = prepare_for_war
		id = "CRO"
		value = 500
	}
	ai_strategy = {
		type = declare_war
		id = "CRO"
